<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Full-year free cash flow will exceed $60<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">0&#160;</font>million</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="3%" bgcolor="#cceeff" style="BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td valign="top" width="82%" bgcolor="#cceeff" style="BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="3%" bgcolor="#cceeff" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid; TEXT-ALIGN: center; BORDER-LEFT: black 2px solid">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#9679;</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="82%" bgcolor="#cceeff" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid; BORDER-RIGHT: black 2px solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Net full-year share buyback expected to be in the range of $500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font>million</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">BROOMFIELD, Colo., </font>October&#160;30, 2014 &#8212; Ball Corporation (NYSE:BLL) today reported third quarter net earnings attributable to the corporation of $147.4&#160;million, or $1.04&#160;per diluted share, on sales of $2.2&#160;billion, compared to $115.2&#160;million, or 78&#160;cents per diluted share, on sales of $2.3&#160;billion in the third quarter of 2013. Third quarter 2014 net earnings include after tax charges of $9.4&#160;million, or 7&#160;cents per diluted share, for business consolidation and other activities.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Results for the first nine months of 2014 were net earnings attributable to the corporation of $394.0&#160;million, or $2.76&#160;per diluted share, on sales of $6.5&#160;billion, compared to $282.3&#160;million, or $1.88&#160;per diluted share, on sales of $6.5&#160;billion in the first nine months of 2013. Year-to-date 2014 net earnings include after tax charges of $40.8&#160;million for business consolidation and debt refinancing costs.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Comparable 2014 earnings per diluted share for the third quarter and year-to-date were $1.10&#160;and $3.04, respectively versus third quarter and year-to-date 2013 comparable earnings per diluted share of $1.00&#160;and $2.42, respectively. Details of comparable segment earnings and business consolidation activities can be found in Notes&#160;1 and 2 to the unaudited consolidated financial statements that accompany this news release.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;As anticipated, volume comparisons in the third quarter were challenging, led by weaker than expected customer demand for our beverage cans in Brazil following the World Cup and for steel food containers in North America,&#8221; said John&#160;A. Hayes, chairman, president and chief executive officer. &#8220;Though we continue to navigate through aluminum premium headwinds in Europe, our focus on global cost containment, exceptional manufacturing performance and a lower effective tax rate led to improved third quarter results.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Page 1</font></div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>

<br>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Metal Beverage Packaging, Americas &amp; Asia</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Metal beverage packaging, Americas and Asia, comparable segment operating earnings were $133.4&#160;million in the third quarter on sales of $1.1&#160;billion, compared to $134.8&#160;million on sales of $1.1&#160;billion in the third quarter of 2013. For the first nine months, comparable segment operating earnings were $400.3&#160;million on sales of $3.2&#160;billion, compared to $364.5&#160;million on sales of $3.2&#160;billion during the same period in 2013.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Comparable segment results were roughly flat versus third quarter 2013, as solid beer and specialty container demand in North America were unable to fully offset mid-teen volume declines in Brazil post-World Cup and ongoing softness for 12-ounce carbonated soft drink containers in the U.S. Volumes in China were up mid-single digits. Relentless focus on cost containment across the segment, progress on additional specialty container investments in the U.S., and improving volume conditions as Brazil enters its summer selling season position the segment for better performance going forward.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Metal Beverage Packaging, Europe</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Metal beverage packaging, Europe, results in the quarter were comparable segment operating earnings of $63.8&#160;million on sales of $489.2&#160;million, compared to $60.5&#160;million on sales of $488.9&#160;million in 2013. Results for the first nine months were comparable segment operating earnings of $193.0&#160;million on sales of $1.5&#160;billion, compared to $143.2&#160;million on sales of $1.4&#160;billion in 2013.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Third quarter comparable results were up slightly with cost savings offsetting higher aluminum premiums and low single-digit volume declines for the segment. Progress continues on the Oss, Netherlands, facility, which will begin additional specialty can production during the second quarter of 2015.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Metal Food &amp; Household Products Packaging</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Metal food and household products packaging results in the third quarter were comparable segment operating earnings of $43.0&#160;million on sales of $450.6&#160;million, compared to $58.4&#160;million in 2013 on sales of $463.6&#160;million. Year-to-date results were comparable segment operating earnings of $119.1&#160;million on sales of $1.2&#160;billion, compared to $140.6&#160;million on sales of $1.2&#160;billion in 2013.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Segment results were down in the quarter influenced by mid-to-upper single-digit volume declines for steel food containers and ongoing service center manufacturing inefficiencies in the U.S. Strong European extruded aluminum performance continues and Ball is initiating investment in India to meet increasing demand for extruded aluminum packaging in that region.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<br>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Aerospace and Technologies</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Aerospace and technologies results were comparable segment operating earnings of $21.2&#160;million on sales of $221.7&#160;million in the third quarter, compared to $18.0&#160;million on sales of $217.5&#160;million in 2013. For the first nine months, comparable segment operating earnings were $70.1&#160;million on sales of $683.5&#160;million compared to $55.0&#160;million on sales of $675.0&#160;million during the same period last year. Backlog at the end of the quarter was $846.1&#160;million.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">During the quarter, WorldView-3, the first multi-payload, super-spectral, high-resolution commercial satellite for earth observations and advanced geospatial data, successfully launched from Vandenberg Air Force Base. The segment continues to position itself to pursue non-traditional growth projects while leveraging its existing capabilities in the government sector.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Outlook</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;Year-to-date we have returned more than $350&#160;million to shareholders in the form of share repurchases and dividends, and we remain confident that free cash flow will exceed $600&#160;million for 2014 after capital spending of approximately $375&#160;million,&#8221; said Scott&#160;C. Morrison, senior vice president and chief financial officer.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;Our third quarter results largely reflected the volume slowdown and current global economic conditions. As we close out the year, we remain confident in our ability to increase EVA dollar generation and achieve our long-term diluted earnings per share growth goal of 10&#160;to 15&#160;percent,&#8221; Hayes said.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">About Ball Corporation</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Ball Corporation supplies innovative, sustainable packaging solutions for beverage, food and household products customers, as well as aerospace and other technologies and services primarily for the U.S. government. Ball Corporation and its subsidiaries employ 14,500&#160;people worldwide and reported 2013 sales of $8.5&#160;billion. For more information, visit <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.ball.com</font>, or connect with us on <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Facebook</font> or <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Twitter</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">This release contains <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;</font>forward-looking<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8221;</font> statements concerning future events and financial performance. Words such as <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;</font>expects,<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8221; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;</font>anticipates,<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8221; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8220;</font>estimates<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8221;</font> and similar expressions identify forward-looking statements. Such statements are subject to risks and uncertainties, which could cause actual results to differ materially from those expressed or implied. The company undertakes no obligation to publicly update or revise any forward-looking statements, whether as a result of new information, future events or otherwise. Key risks and uncertainties are summarized in filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission, including Exhibit&#160;99 in our Form 10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8211;</font>K, which are available on our website and at <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.sec.gov</font>. Factors that might affect: a)&#160;our packaging segments include product demand fluctuations; availability/cost of raw materials; competitive packaging, pricing and substitution; changes in climate and weather; crop yields; competitive activity; failure to achieve productivity improvements or cost reductions; mandatory deposit or other restrictive packaging laws; customer and supplier consolidation, power and supply chain influence; changes in major customer or supplier contracts or loss of a major customer or supplier; political instability and sanctions; and changes in foreign exchange or tax rates; b)&#160;our aerospace segment include funding, authorization, availability and returns of government and commercial contracts; and delays, extensions and technical uncertainties affecting segment contracts; c)&#160;the company as a whole include those listed plus: changes in senior management; successful or unsuccessful acquisitions and divestitures; regulatory action or issues including tax, environmental, health and workplace safety, including U.S. FDA and other actions or public concerns affecting products filled in our containers, or chemicals or substances used in raw materials or in the manufacturing process; technological developments and innovations; litigation; strikes; labor cost changes; rates of return on assets of the company<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#8217;</font>s defined benefit retirement plans; pension changes; uncertainties surrounding the U.S. government budget, sequestration and debt limit; reduced cash flow; ability to achieve cost-out initiatives; interest rates affecting our debt.</font></div>

<td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-STYLE: normal; DISPLAY: inline">2.</font></font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="81%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-STYLE: normal; DISPLAY: inline">Significant Business Consolidation Activities and Other Noncomparable Items</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2014</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Metal Beverage Packaging, Americas and Asia</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The first nine months included charges of $2.0&#160;million ($1.3&#160;million after tax) related to a fire at a metal beverage packaging, Americas facility. The third quarter and first nine months also included net income of $0.8&#160;million ($0.3&#160;million after tax) and net charges of $1.0&#160;million ($0.7&#160;million after tax), respectively, for ongoing costs related to previously closed facilities and other insignificant costs.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">During the first quarter, the company received and recorded compensation of $5.0&#160;million ($3.7&#160;million after tax) for the reimbursement of severance costs incurred in connection with the company&#8217;s closure and relocation of the Shenzhen, China, manufacturing facility in 2013. Also during the first quarter, the company sold its plastic motor oil container and pail manufacturing business in China. The third quarter and first nine months included a loss of $1.1&#160;million ($1.2&#160;million after tax) and $0.3&#160;million ($0.9&#160;million after tax), respectively, in connection with the sale.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Metal Food and Household Products Packaging</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">In the third quarter, the company recorded charges of $3.6&#160;million ($2.2&#160;million after tax) related to a reduction in force to eliminate certain food can production in the Oakdale, California, facility, as well as the completion of a voluntary separation program. The third quarter and first nine months also included charges of $0.8&#160;million ($0.5&#160;million after tax) and $4.1&#160;million ($2.6&#160;million after tax), respectively, for ongoing costs related to previously closed facilities and other insignificant costs.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">During the fourth quarter of 2013, the company announced the closure of its Danville, Illinois, steel aerosol packaging facility in the second half of 2014. The first nine months of 2014 included charges of $3.8&#160;million ($2.4&#160;million after tax) in connection with the announced closure.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Metal Beverage Packaging, Europe, and Corporate</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The third quarter and first nine months included charges of $0.9&#160;million ($0.8&#160;million after tax) and $3.2&#160;million ($2.9&#160;million after tax), respectively, for headcount reductions, cost-out initiatives and the relocation of the company&#8217;s European headquarters from Germany to Switzerland, as well as additional tax expense of $1.9&#160;million and $6.1&#160;million, respectively, related to this relocation. The third quarter and first nine months also included charges of $3.7&#160;million ($3.1&#160;million after tax) and $4.7&#160;million ($4.8&#160;million after tax), respectively, related to the write off of previously capitalized costs associated with the company&#8217;s Lublin, Poland, facility, and for other insignificant activities.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">In January, Ball completed the redemption of its outstanding 7.375&#160;percent senior notes due in September 2019. The redemption of the bonds resulted in a first quarter charge of $33.1&#160;million ($20.6&#160;million after tax) for the call premium and the write off of unamortized financing costs and premiums.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">2013</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">In the third quarter, the company recorded an accounts receivable provision of $27.0&#160;million ($18.0&#160;million after tax, or $0.12&#160;per diluted share) as a result of the financial difficulties of a significant customer. This provision represented the company&#8217;s estimate of the most likely potential loss of value it expected to incur as a result of the financial condition of this customer.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">During July 2013, the company signed a compensation agreement with the Chinese government to vacate the Shenzhen manufacturing facility and relocate the production equipment. The third quarter and first nine months included charges of $6.8&#160;million ($5.1&#160;million after tax) and $8.1&#160;million ($6.1&#160;million after tax), respectively, for closure and relocation costs, which were primarily reimbursed in the fourth quarter 2013 and first quarter 2014.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">In February 2013, Ball announced the closure of its Elgin, Illinois, food and household products packaging facility. The third quarter and first nine months included charges of $1.9&#160;million ($1.2&#160;million after tax) and $28.0&#160;million ($17.0&#160;million after tax), respectively, in connection with the closure.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The third quarter and first nine months included charges of $1.6&#160;million ($1.0&#160;million after tax) and $8.7&#160;million ($5.3&#160;million after tax) to balance regional supply and demand in Ball's metal beverage packaging, Americas, operations. Additionally, the third quarter and first nine months also included charges of $5.3&#160;million ($3.2&#160;million after tax) and $8.4&#160;million ($5.1&#160;million after tax), respectively, related to previously announced closures of Ball's Columbus, Ohio, and Gainesville, Florida, metal beverage packaging, Americas, facilities and related voluntary separation programs.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Page 9</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-STYLE: normal; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Notes to the Condensed Financial Statements (Third Quarter 2014)</font></font></div>

<tr>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="3%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="FONT-STYLE: normal; DISPLAY: inline">2.</font></font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="81%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><font style="DISPLAY: inline"><font style="FONT-STYLE: normal">Significant Business Consolidation Activities and Other Noncomparable Items</font> (continued)</font></font></div>
</td>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Other items in the third quarter and first nine months included charges of $1.7 million ($1.4 million after tax) and $5.5 million ($4.3 million after tax), for the third quarter 2012 relocation of the company's European headquarters from Germany to Switzerland, as well as additional tax expense of $2.0&#160;million and $5.9&#160;million, respectively, related to this relocation. The second quarter and first nine months also included a charge of $5.9&#160;million ($3.6&#160;million after tax) to migrate certain employees from a multi-employer defined benefit pension plan to a Ball-sponsored defined benefit pension plan. Additionally, the first six months included income of $3.5 million ($2.1 million after tax) related to the reimbursement of funds paid in 2012 for the settlement of certain Canadian defined benefit pension liabilities of previously closed facilities.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">During the second quarter, Ball issued $1 billion of 4.00 percent senior notes due in November 2023 and tendered for the redemption of $375 million of 7.125 percent senior notes originally due in September 2016. The redemption of the bonds, as well as the renegotiation of Ball's bank credit facilities in June, resulted in a charge of $26.9 million ($16.3 million after tax) for the call premium and the write off of unamortized financing costs and discounts.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><br>
<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">A summary of the effects of the above transactions on after-tax earnings is as follows:</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 9pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Ball Corporation Board Elects Michael&#160;J. Cave as</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 9pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 18pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">New Member, Declares Quarterly Dividend</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">BROOMFIELD, Colo.,</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"> Oct.&#160;29, 2014 &#8212; </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ball Corporation&#8217;s</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"> (NYSE: BLL) </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">board of directors today elected </font>Michael&#160;J. Cave, retired senior vice president from The Boeing Company, to serve as a director of the Corporation.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Cave served Boeing for 31&#160;years, most recently as president of Boeing Capital Corp., a wholly owned Boeing subsidiary responsible for arranging, structuring and providing financing for Boeing&#8217;s commercial airplane and space and defense products. Prior to that, he served as senior vice president of business development and strategy for the corporation; senior vice president and general manager for Boeing&#8217;s commercial airplane programs; chief financial officer of Boeing Commercial Airplanes, and vice president of finance for Boeing Information, Space &amp; Defense Systems. Cave currently serves on the board of directors for Harley-Davidson, Inc. and Aircastle Limited.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The board also declared a cash dividend of 13&#160;cents per share, payable Dec.&#160;15, 2014, to shareholders of record as of Dec.&#160;1, 2014. Ball will report its third quarter 2014 earnings on Thursday, Oct.&#160;30, 2014. Conference call details are below.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Ball Corporation supplies innovative, sustainable packaging solutions for beverage, food and household products customers, as well as aerospace and other technologies and services primarily for the U.S. government. Ball Corporation and its subsidiaries employ 14,500&#160;people worldwide and reported 2013 sales of $8.5&#160;billion. For more information, visit <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">www.ball.com</font>, or connect with us on <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Facebook</font> or <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Twitter</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block"><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Conference Call Details</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ball Corporation</font> will hold its regular quarterly conference call on the company&#8217;s results and performance on Thursday, Oct.&#160;30, at 9&#160;a.m. Mountain Time (11&#160;a.m. Eastern). The North American toll-free number for the call is 800-909-4197. International callers should dial 303-223-0118. Please use the following URL for a webcast of the live call:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">http://edge.media-server.com/m/p/chheg3e2/lan/en</font></font></div>

To access the replay, call 800-633-8284 (North American callers) or 402-977-9140 (international callers) and use reservation number 21735281.
